<text>Great off-leash dog park with grass! Shade is limited more to one area of the park, but the park is pretty big. There are regular and dog drinking fountains and dog bags provided. Park is well kept and clean and I've had no issues with aggressive dogs while mine are playing here. Only downside is that there is only a fence on part of the park (plenty high to keep them away from the bike path and Silver Strand road) but not one by the residential road. Depending on where you are at in the park, you could be plenty far away from that road, but people with canine "escape artists" might want to check it out first before bringing their pup. There is a baseball park and playground nearby, along with a jogging path. Free parallel street parking is near the edge of the park by the "Dog Run" sign, but there is a free parking lot on the opposite side of the park if preferred.<//text><Rating>5<//Rating><Response>None</Response>< Time>

< review>
Almost a perfect park.

The only reason it's not a five is because of some of the park goers. The dogs are exceptionally nice, most times. However, some of the owners tend to be awkward with their dogs. It sometimes just seems like they're afraid to let their dogs play.

Other positives are that it is easy to access, beautiful scenery, and a cool breeze is almost always present. It's not fenced in, but large with open grass fields. Really, just a nice park.< /review>

<rating>1< /rating>< Text>
The quality of the food, like the portion sizes, has steadily gone down hill. A recent purchase was likely the final purchase from this restaurant. I suspect a great deal of their business is solely because it is the only Chinese restaurant in the area. Since there is no competitive alternative  they take advantage of this unfortunate situation. They lack severely in customer service nor seem to be to concerned about it either. A recent order demonstrated their apathy towards a positive customer experience. Two "large" entrees of the same item were ordered as well as soups for pick up. Upon returning home we were very discouraged and frankly angered that both entree containers were only 2/3 full. The portions are small as it is. Quite obviously intentional  and obviously not a concern as the customer has paid and departed before discovering this deliberate shortage. Shortly thereafter, I telephoned the restaurant only to be informed that there is no manager, no owner in fact not one person present whom is responsible for the management of the restaurant. The repeated response from the unknown employee was simply call back next week. What a poorly run operation. Later that evening I received a telephone call from someone purporting to be the owner. I asked her if she ordered two pizzas for delivery and upon delivery if there was only 2/3 of a pizza in each box how would that be received. Her unconcerned response was simply thanks for the input and good bye. Another example of the lack of customer service and lack of pride in their product.< /Text>

< text>
Good burgers as usual, but minus one star for service with an apparent two-faced, bi-polar attitude. We waited about 5 minutes before anybody noticed us. Cashier finally came out of the kitchen after chatting with the cook, and was  very pleasant when we first came in, but after we paid for our order, she went back into the kitchen and was talking and laughing with the cook again. Not a word about where to wait, just that she would let us know when it was ready. When she came back in a few minutes, and saw we were still standing there, and rather abrasively barked at us to "Hey! wait outside, we can't just have people waiting around in here. Covid, you know." After  stepping outside, we saw a customer who had  been sitting outside at a patio table come in to request a drink refill and the cashier not only served him immediately, but chatted with him for 2-3 minutes after. A warning to all: if you order takeout here, be prepared to step outside IMMEDIATELY after ordering or you will get chewed out. The cashier was  pleasant again when she brought our order, spouting compliments,  but that was little recompense for her attitude earlier. I agree with supporting local small business, but I do NOT agree with poor treatment of customers, and attempting to patronize  them afterward as if nothing happened.<//text>

< text>
Small hole-in-the-wall burger joint next to Takkens. Small menu, mostly burgers & fries. I've visited twice and ordered a double cheeseburger each time, and they were both absolutely delicious. The service was good and they cooked the food fast. As of April 2016, the double cheeseburgers are only $4.85, about the same price as fast food but infinitely tastier. If you're looking for a real, hand pressed burger but don't want to spend a lot, this is the place. Will keep coming, and would recommend to anyone.< /text>
